File: scripts/health-check.py
================
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""System health checks for Claude Code infrastructure.

Modes:
    --mode session-start   Quick checks at session start (<3s). Stdout → Claude context.
    --mode stop            Validate cost CSV row after capture-cost.py. macOS notification on failure.
    --mode full            Comprehensive diagnostics for on-demand /health-check skill.

Silent when healthy (session-start/stop). Always exits 0.
"""

import argparse
import csv
import json
import os
import socket
import subprocess
import sys
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

CLAUDE_DIR = os.path.expanduser("~/.claude")
SETTINGS_JSON = os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "settings.json")
COST_LOG = os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "cost-log.csv")
MCP_JSON = os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "mcp.json")
MLFLOW_DB = os.path.expanduser("~/mlflow.db")
CHECKPOINT_FILE = os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, ".claude-md-checkpoint")
TOKEN_FILE = os.path.expanduser("~/.atlassian-tokens.env")
CONFLUENCE_ENV = os.path.expanduser("~/confluence-mcp-server/.env")

# Thresholds
COST_ANOMALY_MULTIPLIER = 3  # alert if session cost > 3x rolling average
COST_ROLLING_DAYS = 7
COST_MIN_ROWS_FOR_ANOMALY = 5  # need at least this many rows to detect anomalies
LOW_TOKEN_THRESHOLD = 10  # rows with input_tokens < this are suspicious


# ---------- utility ----------

def notify(title: str, body: str = ""):
    """Send a macOS notification."""
    short = body[:200].replace('"', '\\"').replace("\n", " ") if body else ""
    try:
        subprocess.run(
            ["osascript", "-e",
             f'display notification "{short}" with title "Claude Code" subtitle "{title}"'],
            capture_output=True, timeout=5,
        )
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        pass


def port_open(host: str, port: int, timeout: float = 2) -> bool:
    try:
        with socket.create_connection((host, port), timeout=timeout):
            return True
    except (OSError, socket.timeout):
        return False


def curl_ok(url: str, timeout: int = 2) -> bool:
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["curl", "-sf", "--max-time", str(timeout), url],
            capture_output=True, timeout=timeout + 2,
        )
        return r.returncode == 0
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        return False


def docker_running() -> bool:
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(["docker", "info"], capture_output=True, timeout=5)
        return r.returncode == 0
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        return False


def jira_container_up() -> bool:
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["docker", "ps", "--filter", "ancestor=audience-jira-mcp-server",
             "--format", "{{.ID}}"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        return bool(r.stdout.strip())
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        return False


# ---------- cost CSV helpers ----------

def read_cost_rows(max_rows: int = 100) -> list[dict]:
    """Read the last N rows from cost-log.csv."""
    if not os.path.isfile(COST_LOG):
        return []
    try:
        with open(COST_LOG, newline="") as f:
            reader = csv.DictReader(f)
            rows = list(reader)
        return rows[-max_rows:]
    except Exception:
        return []


def last_cost_row() -> dict | None:
    rows = read_cost_rows(1)
    return rows[0] if rows else None


def rolling_average_cost(days: int = COST_ROLLING_DAYS) -> float | None:
    """Compute average session cost over the last N days."""
    rows = read_cost_rows(500)
    if not rows:
        return None

    cutoff = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=days)
    recent = []
    for r in rows:
        try:
            dt = datetime.strptime(r.get("date", ""), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
            cost = float(r.get("cost_usd", 0))
            if dt >= cutoff and cost > 0:
                recent.append(cost)
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            continue

    if len(recent) < COST_MIN_ROWS_FOR_ANOMALY:
        return None
    return sum(recent) / len(recent)


# ---------- checks ----------

class HealthReport:
    def __init__(self):
        self.warnings: list[str] = []
        self.info: list[str] = []

    def warn(self, msg: str):
        self.warnings.append(msg)

    def ok(self, msg: str):
        self.info.append(msg)

    def has_warnings(self) -> bool:
        return len(self.warnings) > 0


# ---------- CLAUDE.md checkpoint ----------

def update_claude_md_checkpoint(report: HealthReport):
    """Write HEAD SHA to checkpoint file if session had no warnings."""
    if report.has_warnings():
        return
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "rev-parse", "HEAD"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            return
        sha = r.stdout.strip()
        # Skip write if SHA unchanged
        if os.path.isfile(CHECKPOINT_FILE):
            with open(CHECKPOINT_FILE) as f:
                if f.read().strip() == sha:
                    return
        with open(CHECKPOINT_FILE, "w") as f:
            f.write(sha + "\n")
    except (OSError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        pass


def detect_claude_md_change() -> str | None:
    """Return a notice string if CLAUDE.md changed since last checkpoint."""
    if not os.path.isfile(CHECKPOINT_FILE):
        return None
    try:
        with open(CHECKPOINT_FILE) as f:
            sha = f.read().strip()
        if not sha:
            return None
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "diff", "--name-only", sha, "HEAD", "--", "CLAUDE.md"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            return None
        if r.stdout.strip():
            return f"CLAUDE.md changed since last verified checkpoint ({sha[:7]})"
    except (OSError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        pass
    return None


def check_vpn(report: HealthReport):
    """Check VPN connectivity by resolving jira.disney.com.

    A 302 from Jira means VPN is disconnected (redirects to SSO), not token expiry.
    Token expiry returns 401. This check prevents misdiagnosis.
    """
    try:
        socket.getaddrinfo("jira.disney.com", 443, socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
    except socket.gaierror:
        report.warn("VPN: jira.disney.com cannot be resolved — VPN is likely disconnected. Connect to VPN before running Jira commands.")
        return

    # DNS resolves, but check if we actually get through (not just cached DNS)
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["curl", "-s", "-o", "/dev/null", "-w", "%{http_code}",
             "--max-time", "5", "https://jira.disney.com/status"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=8,
        )
        code = r.stdout.strip()
        if code == "200":
            report.ok("VPN: connected (jira.disney.com reachable)")
        elif code == "302" or code == "000":
            report.warn("VPN: jira.disney.com returned HTTP " + code + " — VPN is likely disconnected. Connect to VPN before running Jira commands.")
        else:
            report.ok(f"VPN: jira.disney.com reachable (HTTP {code})")
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        report.warn("VPN: jira.disney.com timed out — VPN is likely disconnected")


def check_mlflow(report: HealthReport):
    """Check MLflow server health."""
    if curl_ok("http://127.0.0.1:5001/health"):
        report.ok("MLflow: healthy")
    else:
        report.warn("MLflow is DOWN — traces and cost tags will be lost this session. Run: mlflow server --host 127.0.0.1 --port 5001 --backend-store-uri sqlite:////Users/sameul.nasir/mlflow.db &")


def check_docker_jira(report: HealthReport):
    """Check Docker daemon and Jira container."""
    if not docker_running():
        report.warn("Docker is not running — Jira skills will fail")
        return
    if not jira_container_up():
        report.warn("Jira MCP container is not running — run /connect-jira to start it")
        return
    if not port_open("localhost", 3000):
        report.warn("Jira container is running but port 3000 is not responding")
        return
    report.ok("Docker + Jira container: healthy")


def check_aws_credentials(report: HealthReport):
    """Check AWS credential validity."""
    creds_file = os.path.expanduser("~/.aws/credentials")
    if not os.path.isfile(creds_file):
        report.warn("AWS credentials file not found")
        return

    try:
        with open(creds_file) as f:
            content = f.read()
        # Look for x_security_token_expires in the twdc-bedrock-central profile
        in_profile = False
        expires = None
        for line in content.splitlines():
            if line.strip().startswith("[twdc-bedrock-central]"):
                in_profile = True
                continue
            if in_profile and line.strip().startswith("["):
                break
            if in_profile and "x_security_token_expires" in line:
                expires = line.split("=", 1)[1].strip()
                break

        if not expires:
            # Can't determine TTL, skip check
            return

        # Parse expiry — handle ISO format
        try:
            exp_dt = datetime.fromisoformat(expires.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
            now = datetime.now(exp_dt.tzinfo) if exp_dt.tzinfo else datetime.now()
            ttl = (exp_dt - now).total_seconds()
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return

        if ttl <= 0:
            report.warn("AWS credentials are EXPIRED — Bedrock calls will fail. Refresh with: ca")
        elif ttl < 300:
            minutes = int(ttl / 60)
            report.warn(f"AWS credentials expire in {minutes} min — consider refreshing soon")
        else:
            report.ok(f"AWS credentials: valid ({int(ttl/60)} min remaining)")

    except (OSError, IOError):
        pass


def check_cost_csv_health(report: HealthReport):
    """Check cost CSV for recent issues."""
    if not os.path.isfile(COST_LOG):
        report.warn("Cost log missing — no session costs are being tracked")
        return

    rows = read_cost_rows(10)
    if not rows:
        report.warn("Cost log is empty — cost tracking may be broken")
        return

    # Check last few rows for suspicious data
    empty_count = 0
    for r in rows[-5:]:
        try:
            inp = int(r.get("input_tokens", 0))
            out = int(r.get("output_tokens", 0))
            if inp < LOW_TOKEN_THRESHOLD and out < LOW_TOKEN_THRESHOLD:
                empty_count += 1
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            empty_count += 1

    if empty_count >= 3:
        report.warn(f"Cost tracking may be broken — {empty_count} of last 5 rows have near-zero tokens")
    else:
        report.ok("Cost CSV: recent rows look valid")


def check_cost_anomaly(report: HealthReport):
    """Check if the last session cost was anomalously high."""
    avg = rolling_average_cost()
    if avg is None:
        return  # not enough data

    last = last_cost_row()
    if not last:
        return

    try:
        last_cost = float(last.get("cost_usd", 0))
    except (ValueError, TypeError):
        return

    if last_cost <= 0:
        return

    if last_cost > avg * COST_ANOMALY_MULTIPLIER:
        report.warn(
            f"Last session cost ${last_cost:.2f} is {last_cost/avg:.1f}x your "
            f"{COST_ROLLING_DAYS}-day average (${avg:.2f})"
        )
    else:
        report.ok(f"Cost: last session ${last_cost:.2f} (avg ${avg:.2f})")


def check_mlflow_db(report: HealthReport):
    """Check MLflow SQLite DB exists at the correct absolute path.

    Catches two known issues:
    - 3-slash SQLite URI creating DB in wrong location
    - Missing --backend-store-uri causing silent trace loss
    """
    if not os.path.isfile(MLFLOW_DB):
        report.warn(
            f"MLflow DB not found at {MLFLOW_DB} — traces may be silently lost. "
            "Verify ensure-mlflow.sh uses sqlite:////Users/sameul.nasir/mlflow.db (4 slashes)"
        )
    else:
        report.ok("MLflow DB: exists at correct path")

    # Check for rogue DBs created by 3-slash URI bug
    rogue_paths = [
        os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "mlflow.db"),
        os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "Users"),
    ]
    for rogue in rogue_paths:
        if os.path.exists(rogue):
            report.warn(
                f"Rogue MLflow DB found at {rogue} — likely created by 3-slash SQLite URI. "
                "Merge traces back and delete: sqlite3 wrong.db '.dump trace_info' | sqlite3 right.db"
            )


def check_settings_env_keys(report: HealthReport):
    """Verify MLflow env vars are under 'env' not 'environment' in settings.json.

    Known issue: Claude Code silently ignores variables under an 'environment' key.
    """
    try:
        with open(SETTINGS_JSON) as f:
            settings = json.load(f)
    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
        report.warn("Cannot read settings.json")
        return

    # Check for the wrong key
    if "environment" in settings:
        env_wrong = settings["environment"]
        misplaced = [k for k in env_wrong if "MLFLOW" in k or "ANTHROPIC" in k or "AWS" in k]
        if misplaced:
            report.warn(
                f"settings.json has env vars under 'environment' key (silently ignored): "
                f"{', '.join(misplaced)}. Move them to the 'env' key."
            )
        else:
            report.warn(
                "settings.json has an 'environment' key — Claude Code ignores this. "
                "Use the 'env' key for all environment variables."
            )
        return

    # Verify required MLflow vars are present under env
    env = settings.get("env", {})
    required = ["MLFLOW_TRACKING_URI", "MLFLOW_CLAUDE_TRACING_ENABLED"]
    missing = [k for k in required if k not in env]
    if missing:
        report.warn(f"settings.json 'env' missing: {', '.join(missing)} — tracing may not work")
    else:
        report.ok("settings.json: MLflow env vars correctly under 'env' key")


def check_mlflow_db_traces(report: HealthReport):
    """Verify MLflow DB has traces (catches silent data loss). Full mode only."""
    if not os.path.isfile(MLFLOW_DB):
        return  # Already caught by check_mlflow_db

    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["sqlite3", MLFLOW_DB, "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trace_info;"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode == 0:
            count = int(r.stdout.strip())
            if count == 0:
                report.warn("MLflow DB has 0 traces — traces are being silently lost")
            else:
                report.ok(f"MLflow DB: {count} traces stored")
        else:
            report.warn(f"Cannot query MLflow DB: {r.stderr.strip()}")
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired, ValueError):
        report.warn("Cannot query MLflow DB — sqlite3 not available or timed out")


def check_trace_provenance(report: HealthReport):
    """Verify traces have proper source system identification. Full mode only."""
    if not os.path.isfile(MLFLOW_DB):
        return  # Already caught by check_mlflow_db

    try:
        # Check source system distribution
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["sqlite3", MLFLOW_DB, "SELECT value, COUNT(*) FROM trace_tags WHERE key='system_source' GROUP BY value;"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode == 0 and r.stdout.strip():
            lines = [line.split('|') for line in r.stdout.strip().split('\n') if '|' in line]
            source_counts = {source: int(count) for source, count in lines}
            
            total_tagged = sum(source_counts.values())
            if total_tagged > 0:
                summary = ", ".join([f"{source}: {count}" for source, count in source_counts.items()])
                report.ok(f"Trace provenance: {total_tagged} traces tagged ({summary})")
            else:
                report.warn("No traces have source system tags — provenance tracking not working")
        
        # Check for untagged traces (exclude Cortex imports which store source in request_metadata)
        r2 = subprocess.run(
            ["sqlite3", MLFLOW_DB, """
            SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trace_info ti
            WHERE NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1 FROM trace_tags tt
                WHERE tt.request_id = ti.request_id AND tt.key = 'system_source'
            )
            AND NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1 FROM trace_request_metadata trm
                WHERE trm.request_id = ti.request_id AND trm.key = 'system_source'
            );"""],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r2.returncode == 0:
            untagged = int(r2.stdout.strip())
            if untagged > 0:
                report.warn(f"{untagged} traces missing source system tags")
            
        # Verify current session detection works
        current_source = "cortex_code" if os.environ.get("CORTEX_SESSION_ID") else "claude_code"
        report.ok(f"Current session detected as: {current_source}")
        
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired, ValueError) as e:
        report.warn(f"Cannot verify trace provenance: {e}")


def check_cortex_import(report: HealthReport):
    """Import any new Cortex conversations into MLflow. Full mode only."""
    converter = os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "scripts", "cortex_to_mlflow_converter.py")
    cortex_dir = os.path.expanduser("~/.snowflake/cortex/conversations")

    if not os.path.isfile(converter):
        return
    if not os.path.isdir(cortex_dir):
        return

    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            [sys.executable, converter, "--dry-run"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            report.warn(f"Cortex import dry-run failed: {r.stderr.strip()[:100]}")
            return

        new_count = r.stdout.count("\U0001f195")
        if new_count == 0:
            report.ok("Cortex import: all conversations already in MLflow")
            return

        r2 = subprocess.run(
            [sys.executable, converter],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30,
        )
        if r2.returncode == 0:
            report.ok(f"Cortex import: {new_count} new conversation(s) imported")
        else:
            report.warn(f"Cortex import failed: {r2.stderr.strip()[:100]}")

    except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
        report.warn("Cortex import timed out")
    except Exception as e:
        report.warn(f"Cortex import error: {e}")


def check_legacy_commands(report: HealthReport):
    """Check for leftover files in ~/.claude/commands/ (legacy directory)."""
    commands_dir = os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "commands")
    if not os.path.isdir(commands_dir):
        report.ok("Legacy commands: no commands/ directory")
        return
    # Find any files recursively
    files = []
    for root, _dirs, filenames in os.walk(commands_dir):
        for fname in filenames:
            files.append(os.path.join(root, fname))
    if not files:
        report.ok("Legacy commands: commands/ directory is empty")
    else:
        dirs = sorted({os.path.basename(os.path.dirname(f)) for f in files})
        report.warn(
            f"Legacy commands: {len(files)} file(s) in commands/ ({', '.join(dirs)}) — "
            f"these should be migrated to skills/ or removed"
        )


def check_git_status(report: HealthReport):
    """Check for uncommitted files in ~/.claude/ repo. Full mode only."""
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "status", "--porcelain"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            return  # Not a git repo or git error — skip silently

        lines = [l for l in r.stdout.strip().splitlines() if l.strip()]
        if not lines:
            report.ok("Git: working tree clean")
        else:
            # Categorize: untracked vs modified
            untracked = [l for l in lines if l.startswith("??")]
            modified = [l for l in lines if not l.startswith("??")]
            parts = []
            if untracked:
                parts.append(f"{len(untracked)} untracked")
            if modified:
                parts.append(f"{len(modified)} modified")
            report.warn(f"Git: {', '.join(parts)} file(s) not committed in ~/.claude/")
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        pass


def check_git_sync(report: HealthReport):
    """Check if ~/.claude/ repo is synced with remote. Full mode only."""
    try:
        # Check if git repo exists
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "rev-parse", "--git-dir"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            return  # Not a git repo — skip silently
        
        # Check if we have a remote configured
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "remote", "get-url", "origin"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            report.warn("Git: No remote 'origin' configured")
            return
            
        remote_url = r.stdout.strip()
        
        # Fetch latest from remote (with timeout)
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "fetch", "origin"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            # Network/auth failure - report but don't fail
            report.warn("Git: Failed to fetch from remote (network/auth issue)")
            return
            
        # Check current branch
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "branch", "--show-current"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0 or not r.stdout.strip():
            report.warn("Git: Not on a trackable branch (detached HEAD)")
            return
            
        current_branch = r.stdout.strip()
        
        # Check if branch tracks remote
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "rev-parse", "--abbrev-ref", f"{current_branch}@{{upstream}}"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            report.warn(f"Git: Branch '{current_branch}' does not track remote")
            return
            
        # Compare local vs remote
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["git", "-C", CLAUDE_DIR, "rev-list", "--left-right", "--count", f"{current_branch}...origin/{current_branch}"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            report.warn("Git: Could not compare with remote branch")
            return
            
        counts = r.stdout.strip().split()
        if len(counts) != 2:
            return
            
        ahead_count = int(counts[0])
        behind_count = int(counts[1])
        
        if ahead_count == 0 and behind_count == 0:
            repo_name = remote_url.split('/')[-1].replace('.git', '')
            report.ok(f"Git: In sync with {repo_name}")
        elif behind_count > 0 and ahead_count == 0:
            report.warn(f"Git: {behind_count} commit(s) behind remote (auto-pull will sync on next session)")
        elif ahead_count > 0 and behind_count == 0:
            report.warn(f"Git: {ahead_count} commit(s) ahead of remote (run: cd ~/.claude && git push)")
        else:
            report.warn(f"Git: Diverged from remote ({ahead_count} ahead, {behind_count} behind)")
            
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired, ValueError):
        pass


def jira_sse_healthy() -> bool:
    """Check if the Jira SSE endpoint is responding."""
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["curl", "-s", "-o", "/dev/null", "-w", "%{http_code}",
             "--max-time", "3", "http://localhost:3000/sse"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        return r.stdout.strip() == "200"
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        return False


def get_jira_container_id() -> str | None:
    """Get the running Jira container ID."""
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["docker", "ps", "--filter", "ancestor=audience-jira-mcp-server",
             "--format", "{{.ID}}"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        return r.stdout.strip() or None
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        return None


def get_jira_token_from_container(container_id: str) -> str | None:
    """Extract the JIRA_TOKEN env var from the running container."""
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["docker", "exec", container_id, "printenv", "JIRA_TOKEN"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5,
        )
        return r.stdout.strip() or None
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        return None


def container_has_sse_patch(container_id: str) -> bool:
    """Check if the _read_stream_writers leak patch exists in the container's sse.py."""
    sse_path = "/usr/local/lib/python3.12/site-packages/mcp/server/sse.py"
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["docker", "exec", container_id, "grep", "-q",
             "_read_stream_writers.pop", sse_path],
            capture_output=True, timeout=5,
        )
        return r.returncode == 0
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        return False


def read_token_from_file(key: str) -> str | None:
    """Read a token from ~/.atlassian-tokens.env."""
    if not os.path.isfile(TOKEN_FILE):
        return None
    try:
        with open(TOKEN_FILE) as f:
            for line in f:
                line = line.strip()
                if line.startswith(f"{key}="):
                    return line.split("=", 1)[1].strip() or None
    except OSError:
        pass
    return None


def read_confluence_token() -> str | None:
    """Read the Confluence token from ~/confluence-mcp-server/.env or token file."""
    # Try .env file first
    if os.path.isfile(CONFLUENCE_ENV):
        try:
            with open(CONFLUENCE_ENV) as f:
                for line in f:
                    line = line.strip()
                    if line.startswith("CONFLUENCE_TOKEN="):
                        return line.split("=", 1)[1].strip() or None
        except OSError:
            pass
    # Fallback to token file
    return read_token_from_file("CONFLUENCE_TOKEN")


def check_token_store(report: HealthReport):
    """Verify ~/.atlassian-tokens.env exists with non-empty entries."""
    if not os.path.isfile(TOKEN_FILE):
        report.warn("Token store missing (~/.atlassian-tokens.env) — run /update-atlassian-token to create it")
        return

    tokens = {}
    try:
        with open(TOKEN_FILE) as f:
            for line in f:
                line = line.strip()
                if "=" in line and not line.startswith("#"):
                    key, val = line.split("=", 1)
                    if val.strip():
                        tokens[key.strip()] = val.strip()
    except OSError:
        report.warn("Token store: cannot read ~/.atlassian-tokens.env")
        return

    missing = []
    if "JIRA_TOKEN" not in tokens:
        missing.append("JIRA_TOKEN")
    if "CONFLUENCE_TOKEN" not in tokens:
        missing.append("CONFLUENCE_TOKEN")

    if missing:
        report.warn(f"Token store: missing {', '.join(missing)} in ~/.atlassian-tokens.env")
    else:
        report.ok("Token store: both tokens present")


def check_token_expiry(report: HealthReport):
    """Check PAT expiry for Jira and Confluence tokens."""
    services = {
        "jira": {
            "host": "jira.disney.com",
            "url": "https://jira.disney.com/rest/pat/latest/tokens",
            "token": None,
        },
        "confluence": {
            "host": "confluence.disney.com",
            "url": "https://confluence.disney.com/rest/pat/latest/tokens",
            "token": None,
        },
    }

    # Get Jira token: try container first, then token file
    container_id = get_jira_container_id()
    if container_id:
        services["jira"]["token"] = get_jira_token_from_container(container_id)
    if not services["jira"]["token"]:
        services["jira"]["token"] = read_token_from_file("JIRA_TOKEN")

    # Get Confluence token
    services["confluence"]["token"] = read_confluence_token()

    for svc_name, svc in services.items():
        token = svc["token"]
        if not token:
            report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} — no token available to check")
            continue

        # Check VPN first
        try:
            socket.getaddrinfo(svc["host"], 443, socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
        except socket.gaierror:
            report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} — cannot reach {svc['host']} (VPN?)")
            continue

        try:
            r = subprocess.run(
                ["curl", "-sf", "--max-time", "10",
                 "-H", f"Authorization: Bearer {token}",
                 svc["url"]],
                capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=15,
            )
            if r.returncode != 0 or not r.stdout.strip():
                report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} — could not query PAT API")
                continue

            import json as json_mod
            tokens_data = json_mod.loads(r.stdout)
            if not tokens_data:
                report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} — no PATs found")
                continue

            best = max(tokens_data, key=lambda t: t.get("lastAuthenticatedAt", t.get("lastAccessedAt", "")))
            pat_name = best.get("name", "unknown")
            expiring_at = best.get("expiringAt")

            if not expiring_at:
                report.ok(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} PAT \"{pat_name}\": no expiry set")
                continue

            exp_dt = datetime.fromisoformat(expiring_at.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
            now = datetime.now(exp_dt.tzinfo) if exp_dt.tzinfo else datetime.now()
            days = (exp_dt - now).days
            exp_str = exp_dt.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")

            if days < 0:
                report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} PAT \"{pat_name}\": EXPIRED ({exp_str})")
            elif days < 2:
                report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} PAT \"{pat_name}\": expires {exp_str} ({days} days!) — regenerate NOW")
            elif days < 7:
                report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} PAT \"{pat_name}\": expires {exp_str} ({days} days) — regenerate soon")
            else:
                report.ok(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} PAT \"{pat_name}\": expires {exp_str} ({days} days)")

        except (subprocess.TimeoutExpired, FileNotFoundError, ValueError, KeyError):
            report.warn(f"Token Expiry: {svc_name.capitalize()} — check failed")


def restart_jira_container(report: HealthReport) -> bool:
    """Restart the Jira MCP container, preserving the existing token.

    Returns True if restart succeeded and SSE is healthy.
    """
    container_id = get_jira_container_id()
    if not container_id:
        report.warn("Jira liveness: no container to restart")
        return False

    token = get_jira_token_from_container(container_id)
    if not token:
        # Fallback to persistent token file
        token = read_token_from_file("JIRA_TOKEN")
    if not token:
        report.warn("Jira liveness: could not extract token from container or ~/.atlassian-tokens.env — manual restart needed")
        return False

    # Stop and remove old container
    try:
        subprocess.run(["docker", "stop", container_id], capture_output=True, timeout=15)
        subprocess.run(["docker", "rm", container_id], capture_output=True, timeout=5)
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        report.warn("Jira liveness: failed to stop old container")
        return False

    # Start new container with same token
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(
            ["docker", "run", "-d", "-p", "3000:3000",
             "-e", f"JIRA_TOKEN={token}",
             "-e", "JIRA_URL=https://jira.disney.com",
             "-e", "MCP_TRANSPORT=sse",
             "-e", "MCP_PORT=3000",
             "audience-jira-mcp-server"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=15,
        )
        if r.returncode != 0:
            report.warn(f"Jira liveness: docker run failed — {r.stderr.strip()}")
            return False
    except (FileNotFoundError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):
        report.warn("Jira liveness: docker run timed out")
        return False

    # Poll for SSE to come up — container validates token at startup which can take 30s+
    for attempt in range(6):
        time.sleep(5)
        if jira_sse_healthy():
            report.ok("Jira MCP: auto-restarted container — SSE now healthy")
            return True

    report.warn("Jira liveness: restarted container but SSE not responding after 30s")
    return False


def check_jira_auth(report: HealthReport):
    """Verify Jira SSE endpoint is healthy. Auto-restart container if unhealthy."""
    if not port_open("localhost", 3000):
        return  # Container not running — already caught by check_docker_jira

    if jira_sse_healthy():
        report.ok("Jira MCP: SSE endpoint responding")
        return

    # SSE is down — try auto-restart before reporting failure
    report.ok("Jira MCP: SSE unhealthy — attempting auto-restart")
    if not restart_jira_container(report):
        report.warn(
            "Jira MCP: SSE endpoint not responding after restart. "
            "Token may be expired — refresh at https://jira.disney.com/secure/ViewProfile.jspa"
        )


def check_sse_leak_patch(report: HealthReport):
    """Verify the _read_stream_writers leak patch is present (verification only, no writes).

    The MCP library's SseServerTransport never removes session entries from
    _read_stream_writers on disconnect, causing unbounded dict growth. The fix
    is baked into the Docker image at build time. This check only verifies
    the patch is present — it never writes to site-packages or containers.
    """
    import glob as globmod

    # Check local site-packages
    candidates = globmod.glob(
        os.path.expanduser("~/Library/Python/*/lib/python/site-packages/mcp/server/sse.py")
    )
    if candidates:
        sse_path = candidates[0]
        try:
            with open(sse_path) as f:
                content = f.read()
            if "_read_stream_writers.pop(session_id" in content:
                report.ok("MCP SSE leak patch: applied (local)")
            else:
                report.warn(
                    f"MCP SSE leak patch missing in {sse_path} — "
                    "reinstall mcp with the patch or wait for upstream fix"
                )
        except OSError:
            pass

    # Check the running Jira container (patch should be baked into the image)
    container_id = get_jira_container_id()
    if container_id:
        if container_has_sse_patch(container_id):
            report.ok("MCP SSE leak patch: applied (container)")
        else:
            report.warn(
                "MCP SSE leak patch missing in container — "
                "rebuild Docker image: cd ~/audience-jira-mcp-server && ./build_docker_image.sh"
            )


def check_mcp_dependencies(report: HealthReport):
    """Check MCP server dependencies exist on disk."""
    try:
        with open(MCP_JSON) as f:
            config = json.load(f)
    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
        report.warn("Cannot read mcp.json")
        return

    servers = config.get("mcpServers", {})
    for name, conf in servers.items():
        # SSE servers — check URL reachability
        if "url" in conf:
            url = conf["url"].rstrip("/sse").rstrip("/")
            if port_open("localhost", 3000) if "3000" in url else curl_ok(url):
                report.ok(f"MCP {name}: endpoint reachable")
            else:
                report.warn(f"MCP {name}: endpoint {url} not reachable")
            continue

        # stdio servers — check command exists
        cmd = conf.get("command")
        if cmd:
            import shutil
            if not shutil.which(cmd):
                report.warn(f"MCP {name}: command '{cmd}' not found in PATH")
                continue

        # Check local repo paths in args
        args = conf.get("args", [])
        for arg in args:
            if arg.startswith("/") and ("/" in arg[1:]):
                # Looks like a file path
                if not os.path.exists(arg):
                    report.warn(f"MCP {name}: path not found: {arg}")
                    break
        else:
            report.ok(f"MCP {name}: dependencies present")


def check_cost_trends(report: HealthReport):
    """Compute cost trends for full report."""
    rows = read_cost_rows(500)
    if not rows:
        report.ok("Cost trends: no data")
        return

    now = datetime.now()
    buckets = {"today": [], "7d": [], "30d": []}

    for r in rows:
        try:
            dt = datetime.strptime(r.get("date", ""), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
            cost = float(r.get("cost_usd", 0))
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            continue

        age = (now - dt).days
        if age == 0:
            buckets["today"].append(cost)
        if age <= 7:
            buckets["7d"].append(cost)
        if age <= 30:
            buckets["30d"].append(cost)

    parts = []
    for label, costs in buckets.items():
        if costs:
            total = sum(costs)
            parts.append(f"{label}: ${total:.2f} ({len(costs)} sessions)")
    if parts:
        report.ok(f"Cost trends: {' | '.join(parts)}")


# ---------- stop mode: validate last cost row ----------

def validate_stop(report: HealthReport):
    """Validate the cost row that was just written by capture-cost.py."""
    # Read stdin (Stop hook JSON) but we don't need it
    try:
        sys.stdin.read()
    except Exception:
        pass

    last = last_cost_row()
    if not last:
        report.warn("No cost row found after session — capture-cost.py may have failed")
        return

    # Check if the row was written recently (within last 30 seconds)
    try:
        row_time = datetime.strptime(last.get("date", ""), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        age = (datetime.now() - row_time).total_seconds()
        if age > 30:
            report.warn("Last cost row is stale — capture-cost.py may not have written this session")
            return
    except (ValueError, TypeError):
        report.warn("Last cost row has invalid date")
        return

    # Check for empty/zero tokens
    try:
        inp = int(last.get("input_tokens", 0))
        out = int(last.get("output_tokens", 0))
        cost = float(last.get("cost_usd", 0))
    except (ValueError, TypeError):
        report.warn("Last cost row has non-numeric values — CSV may be corrupted")
        return

    if inp < LOW_TOKEN_THRESHOLD and out < LOW_TOKEN_THRESHOLD:
        report.warn(
            f"Cost row looks empty (input={inp}, output={out}) — "
            "transcript parsing may have failed"
        )
        return

    if cost <= 0 and (inp > 100 or out > 100):
        report.warn(f"Cost is $0 but tokens are non-zero (in={inp}, out={out}) — pricing calculation may be broken")
        return

    # Check for cost anomaly
    avg = rolling_average_cost()
    if avg and cost > avg * COST_ANOMALY_MULTIPLIER:
        report.warn(f"Session cost ${cost:.2f} is {cost/avg:.1f}x your {COST_ROLLING_DAYS}-day average (${avg:.2f})")


# ---------- mode runners ----------

def run_session_start() -> int:
    """Quick checks at session start. Warnings go to stdout → Claude context."""
    report = HealthReport()
    change_notice = detect_claude_md_change()

    check_vpn(report)
    check_mlflow(report)
    check_mlflow_db(report)
    check_settings_env_keys(report)
    check_sse_leak_patch(report)
    check_docker_jira(report)
    check_jira_auth(report)
    check_token_store(report)
    check_aws_credentials(report)
    check_cost_csv_health(report)
    check_cost_anomaly(report)

    if report.has_warnings():
        print("=== HEALTH WARNINGS ===")
        for w in report.warnings:
            print(f"WARNING: {w}")
    # Silent when healthy — no output means no context pollution

    if change_notice:
        print(change_notice)

    update_claude_md_checkpoint(report)

    return 0


def run_stop() -> int:
    """Validate cost row after capture-cost.py. macOS notification on failure."""
    report = HealthReport()
    validate_stop(report)

    if report.has_warnings():
        for w in report.warnings:
            print(f"[health] {w}", file=sys.stderr)
            notify("Cost Tracking Issue", w)

    return 0


def run_skill_validation() -> tuple[list[str], list[str], list[str]]:
    """Run test-skills.py and parse results. Returns (passes, warns, fails)."""
    test_script = os.path.join(CLAUDE_DIR, "scripts", "test-skills.py")
    if not os.path.isfile(test_script):
        return [], ["test-skills.py not found"], []

    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            ["python3", test_script],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30,
        )
    except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
        return [], ["Skill validation timed out"], []

    # Parse the output for individual results
    passes, warns, fails = [], [], []
    for line in result.stdout.splitlines():
        stripped = line.strip()
        if "[PASS]" in stripped:
            # Extract skill name and message after it
            passes.append(stripped.split("[PASS]")[-1].strip().replace("\033[0m", ""))
        elif "[WARN]" in stripped:
            warns.append(stripped.split("[WARN]")[-1].strip().replace("\033[0m", "").replace("\033[33m", ""))
        elif "[FAIL]" in stripped:
            fails.append(stripped.split("[FAIL]")[-1].strip().replace("\033[0m", "").replace("\033[31m", ""))

    return passes, warns, fails


def print_section(title: str, report: HealthReport):
    """Print a section with OK/WARN items."""
    print(f"\n{title}:")
    for item in report.info:
        print(f"   OK  {item}")
    for item in report.warnings:
        print(f"  WARN {item}")


def run_full() -> int:
    """Comprehensive diagnostics for /health-check skill."""
    all_warnings = []

    print("=== System Health Check ===")

    # Infrastructure
    report = HealthReport()
    check_vpn(report)
    check_mlflow(report)
    check_mlflow_db(report)
    check_mlflow_db_traces(report)
    check_trace_provenance(report)
    check_cortex_import(report)
    check_settings_env_keys(report)
    check_sse_leak_patch(report)
    check_docker_jira(report)
    check_jira_auth(report)
    check_token_store(report)
    check_aws_credentials(report)
    print_section("Infrastructure", report)
    all_warnings.extend(report.warnings)

    # Token Expiry
    report = HealthReport()
    check_token_expiry(report)
    print_section("Token Expiry", report)
    all_warnings.extend(report.warnings)

    # MCP Servers
    report = HealthReport()
    check_mcp_dependencies(report)
    print_section("MCP Servers", report)
    all_warnings.extend(report.warnings)

    # Cost Tracking
    report = HealthReport()
    check_cost_csv_health(report)
    check_cost_anomaly(report)
    check_cost_trends(report)
    print_section("Cost Tracking", report)
    all_warnings.extend(report.warnings)

    # Git & Filesystem
    report = HealthReport()
    check_legacy_commands(report)
    check_git_status(report)
    check_git_sync(report)
    print_section("Git & Filesystem", report)
    all_warnings.extend(report.warnings)

    # Skill Validation
    print("\nSkills:")
    passes, warns, fails = run_skill_validation()
    for f in fails:
        print(f"  FAIL {f}")
        all_warnings.append(f"Skill FAIL: {f}")
    for w in warns:
        print(f"  WARN {w}")
    if passes and not fails:
        print(f"   OK  {len(passes)} checks passed across {len(set(p.split()[0] for p in passes))} skills")
    if warns:
        all_warnings.extend(f"Skill WARN: {w}" for w in warns)

    # Summary
    print(f"\n{'=' * 40}")
    if all_warnings:
        print(f"RESULT: {len(all_warnings)} issue(s) found")
        for w in all_warnings:
            print(f"  - {w}")
    else:
        print("RESULT: All systems healthy")

    return 1 if any("FAIL" in w for w in all_warnings) else 0


# ---------- main ----------

def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Claude Code health checks")
    parser.add_argument(
        "--mode", choices=["session-start", "stop", "full"],
        default="full", help="Check mode",
    )
    args = parser.parse_args()

    if args.mode == "session-start":
        return run_session_start()
    elif args.mode == "stop":
        return run_stop()
    else:
        return run_full()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

# Jira Ticket Finder

Find Jira tickets by preset or custom filter, export to CSV, and optionally update a Google Sheet.

**Routing:** Check `$ARGUMENTS` to select a preset:
- `active` (or empty) → Active tickets in current sprint
- `completed` → Completed tickets in current sprint
- `report` → Full sprint overview with risk analysis across all boards
- `hulu-m360` → Hulu Media360 tickets in DSACQ Refined and Ready sprint
- `custom` → Ask user for projects, statuses, sprint, keyword, extra fields, and sheet ID

## Preset Table

| Preset | Projects | Statuses | Sprint | Keyword | Extra Fields | Sheet ID |
|--------|----------|----------|--------|---------|-------------|----------|
| `active` | DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS | Open, In Progress, In Review, In Development, Code Review, Ready for QA, In QA, To Do, Blocked, Reopened, Ready for Development | openSprints() | — | — | `1KMuH8E3YZfwJF0DE7jlk1xTf5SInNgprBcD9523ayBA` |
| `completed` | DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS | Done, Closed, Resolved | openSprints() | — | resolutiondate, customfield_10106 (Story Points) | `1stbT7rh_dKpxJX66Pv1XcOdKkPLFyRtnfTfnmT-d8kE` |
| `report` | DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS | (all non-done) | openSprints() | — | customfield_10106, customfield_10101, updated | — (CSV only) |
| `hulu-m360` | DSACQ | (any) | "DSACQ Refined and Ready" | "Hulu Media360" | — | — (CSV only) |

## Google Sheet References

| Preset | Sheet Name | Sheet ID | URL |
|--------|-----------|----------|-----|
| `active` | Active Sprint Tickets — 2026-02-17 | `1KMuH8E3YZfwJF0DE7jlk1xTf5SInNgprBcD9523ayBA` | https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1KMuH8E3YZfwJF0DE7jlk1xTf5SInNgprBcD9523ayBA/edit |
| `completed` | Completed Sprint Tickets — 2026-02-25 | `1stbT7rh_dKpxJX66Pv1XcOdKkPLFyRtnfTfnmT-d8kE` | https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1stbT7rh_dKpxJX66Pv1XcOdKkPLFyRtnfTfnmT-d8kE/edit |

**Primary method:** Bash with `python3` calling the Jira REST API directly.
**Fallback:** MCP Jira tools (only if the primary method fails entirely).

## Step 1: Verify Connection

Check the Docker container is running and extract the Jira token:

```bash
CONTAINER_ID=$(docker ps -q --filter ancestor=audience-jira-mcp-server)
if [ -z "$CONTAINER_ID" ]; then
  echo "ERROR: audience-jira-mcp-server container is not running. Run /connect-jira first."
  exit 1
fi
JIRA_TOKEN=$(docker exec "$CONTAINER_ID" printenv JIRA_TOKEN)
```

Quick-test the API:

```bash
curl -sf --max-time 10 \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $JIRA_TOKEN" \
  "https://jira.disney.com/rest/api/2/myself" > /dev/null
```

If the container is not running, tell the user to run `/connect-jira` and stop. If the API returns 401, tell the user their token has expired.

## Step 2: Query Tickets and Export CSV

Determine the preset from `$ARGUMENTS` (default: `active`). Scripts live in this skill's directory.

### For `active` or `completed` presets:

```bash
python3 ~/.claude/skills/jira-ticket-finder/query.py active
# or
python3 ~/.claude/skills/jira-ticket-finder/query.py completed
```

See [query.py](query.py) for the full script. It handles: JQL construction, paginated search, sprint name parsing, epic name resolution, URL conversion, CSV export to `~/Desktop/`, and summary display.

### For `report` preset:

```bash
python3 ~/.claude/skills/jira-ticket-finder/query_report.py
```

See [query_report.py](query_report.py) for the full script. It fetches active sprints for all 3 boards (DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS), pulls all tickets, and separates breakout epics (configured in `BREAKOUT_EPICS` dict) from regular board tickets. Displays per-board overview tables grouped by assignee, a dedicated FiveTran Migration section with its own overview and risk analysis, then per-board risk analysis for remaining tickets. Risk scoring factors: status, size, time pressure, staleness, and assignment. Exports CSV to `~/Desktop/` with an `Epic` column.

After the script output, re-display the full report in markdown with:
1. **Overall summary table** at the top (per-section: Total, Done, Remaining, High Risk, Medium Risk) plus top concerns with linked ticket keys
2. **Per-board overview tables** (assignee breakdown)
3. **FiveTran Migration section** — dedicated overview table + risk analysis
4. **Per-board risk analysis** — separate HIGH/MEDIUM risk tables for DSACQ (non-migration), MEOW, QMDS
5. Risk tables include columns: Key (linked), Summary, Status, Assignee, Pts, Why
6. All ticket keys rendered as Jira links: `[KEY](https://jira.disney.com/browse/KEY)`

### For `hulu-m360` preset:

The hulu-m360 preset uses a two-step process — `curl -G` to fetch (handles quoted sprint name and keyword), then a Python script to parse.

**Step 2a: Fetch from Jira**

```bash
JIRA_TOKEN=$(docker exec $(docker ps -q --filter ancestor=audience-jira-mcp-server) printenv JIRA_TOKEN) && \
curl -s --max-time 30 -G \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $JIRA_TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  --data-urlencode 'jql=project = DSACQ AND sprint = "DSACQ Refined and Ready" AND summary ~ "\"Hulu Media360\"" ORDER BY key DESC' \
  --data-urlencode 'fields=summary,status,assignee,priority,issuetype,customfield_10105,customfield_10103,customfield_10101' \
  --data-urlencode 'maxResults=100' \
  "https://jira.disney.com/rest/api/2/search" -o /tmp/hulu_m360_results.json
```

**Step 2b: Parse, resolve epics, export CSV, display summary**

```bash
python3 ~/.claude/skills/jira-ticket-finder/query_hulu_m360.py
```

See [query_hulu_m360.py](query_hulu_m360.py) for the full script. It reads `/tmp/hulu_m360_results.json`, resolves epic names, exports CSV, and displays a summary table.

## Step 3: Update Google Sheet

**Only for `active` and `completed` presets** (hulu-m360 is CSV-only).

After the Python script completes and the CSV is exported, update the Google Sheet with the latest data:

1. **Clear existing data** using `mcp__universal-doc__clear_spreadsheet_range` with URI `doc://google/spreadsheet/{sheet_id}` and range `A1:{last_col}5000`
2. **Write new data** using `mcp__universal-doc__write_spreadsheet_range` with the same URI, range `A1:{last_col}{row_count+1}`, and the full data array (header row + all ticket rows)

| Preset | Sheet ID | Columns | Range |
|--------|----------|---------|-------|
| `active` | `1KMuH8E3YZfwJF0DE7jlk1xTf5SInNgprBcD9523ayBA` | A–J (10 cols) | `A1:J{n}` |
| `completed` | `1stbT7rh_dKpxJX66Pv1XcOdKkPLFyRtnfTfnmT-d8kE` | A–L (12 cols) | `A1:L{n}` |

Build the values array from the CSV output — each row should be a list of string values matching the column order.

## Guidelines

- **Always verify Docker + Jira connectivity before querying.** A failed query with no container running produces confusing Python errors. Check Step 1 first, every time.
- **Use the primary method (Bash + Python + curl) by default.** MCP Jira tools are the fallback only if the primary method fails entirely. The primary method is faster and more reliable.
- **At sprint start, the `completed` preset may return empty results.** This is expected — no tickets are completed yet. For the previous sprint's completions, modify the JQL to use `closedSprints()` or a specific sprint ID.
- **Never hardcode sprint IDs in the skill.** Use `openSprints()` for active/completed presets and named sprint strings for hulu-m360. Sprint IDs change every 2 weeks.
- **Google Sheets updates are only for `active` and `completed` presets.** The hulu-m360 preset is CSV-only. Don't attempt to write to a sheet for hulu-m360.
- **If epic names are missing**, the skill resolves them via Epic Link. If resolution fails (network timeout, permission), show the Epic Link key as a fallback — don't leave it blank.
- **CSV is always exported to `~/Desktop/`.** Don't change the export path — the user expects files there.

---

## Examples

### Example 1: Active Tickets (Default)

**User**: `/jira-ticket-finder` or `/jira-ticket-finder active`

**Claude does**:
1. Verifies Docker container and Jira API connectivity
2. Runs the `active` preset — queries DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS for open sprint tickets
3. Exports CSV to `~/Desktop/active_sprint_tickets_2026-03-04.csv`
4. Updates the Active Sprint Tickets Google Sheet
5. Displays summary: "32 active tickets (DSACQ: 18, MEOW: 8, QMDS: 6) across 7 statuses. CSV exported and Google Sheet updated."

### Example 2: Sprint Report with Risk Analysis

**User**: `/jira-ticket-finder report` or "jira report" or "what needs my attention in jira"

**Claude does**:
1. Verifies Docker container and Jira API connectivity
2. Runs `query_report.py` — fetches active sprints for DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS
3. Re-displays the full report in markdown with linked ticket keys:
   - **Overall summary table** — per-section breakdown (FiveTran Migration, DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS) with Total/Done/Remaining/High/Medium counts, plus top concerns with linked tickets
   - **Per-board overview tables** — assignee breakdown (In Progress, Review, Open, Done, Blocked, Points)
   - **FiveTran Migration section** — dedicated overview table + HIGH/MEDIUM risk tables
   - **Per-board risk analysis** — separate HIGH/MEDIUM risk tables for DSACQ (non-migration), MEOW, QMDS
   - Risk tables include columns: Key (linked), Summary, Status, Assignee, Pts, Why
4. Exports CSV to `~/Desktop/sprint_report_2026-03-16.csv` with Epic column

### Example 3: Hulu Media360 Backlog

**User**: `/jira-ticket-finder hulu-m360`

**Claude does**:
1. Verifies connectivity
2. Runs the `hulu-m360` preset — queries DSACQ for "Hulu Media360" in the Refined and Ready sprint
3. Exports CSV to `~/Desktop/hulu_m360_refined_ready_2026-03-04.csv` (no Google Sheet update for this preset)
4. Displays: "14 Hulu Media360 tickets in Refined and Ready. By status: Open (8), In Progress (4), To Do (2)."

---

## Custom Field Reference

| Field | Custom Field ID | Notes |
|-------|----------------|-------|
| Sprint | `customfield_10105` | List of sprint strings; parse `name=` from the `state=ACTIVE` entry |
| Epic Name | `customfield_10103` | Often `null` — resolve via Epic Link if empty |
| Epic Link | `customfield_10101` | The key of the parent Epic issue (e.g., `DSACQ-1234`) |
| Story Points | `customfield_10106` | Numeric field; may be `null` for unestimated tickets (completed preset only) |

## Key Details

- **hulu-m360 sprint name:** `DSACQ Refined and Ready` (a FUTURE-state sprint used as a backlog/queue, not an active sprint)
- **hulu-m360 JQL uses** `sprint = "DSACQ Refined and Ready"` (sprint name filter, not status)
- **hulu-m360 summary filter:** exact phrase `"Hulu Media360"` using `summary ~ "\"Hulu Media360\""`
- **Important for hulu-m360:** Use `curl -G` with `--data-urlencode` to avoid URL encoding issues. Save results to `/tmp/hulu_m360_results.json` first, then process with a separate `python3` heredoc script.

## Error Handling

| Error | Cause | Action |
|-------|-------|--------|
| Container not running | Docker container stopped | Tell user to run `/connect-jira` |
| `401 Unauthorized` | Token expired or invalid | Tell user to regenerate their Jira Personal Access Token |
| `Connection refused` / timeout | VPN not connected or Jira down | Tell user to check VPN connection |
| Empty results | JQL matches no issues | Verify sprint is active and project keys/status names are correct |
| Empty results at sprint start | No completed tickets yet | For `completed` preset, modify JQL to use `closedSprints()` or a specific sprint ID |

# Outlook Workflow

## Auth Check First

Before any Outlook operation, verify auth: `outlook auth status`
If not authenticated or operations fail unexpectedly, always use `--no-cache`: `! outlook auth login --no-cache`
Never retry auth without `--no-cache` — stale cached tokens are the most common failure mode. See `memory/tools/cli-universe.md` for full troubleshooting.

## Filtering Rules

When presenting emails to the user, always exclude:
- **Jira notifications** — any email from `jira@jira.email.twdctech.com` or with `[JIRA]` in the subject
- **Meeting updates** — calendar invites, cancellations, updates (e.g., "Canceled:", recurring meeting series updates)
- **Digests** — Daily Digest, Weekly Digest, or similar automated roundup emails
- **dev-portal** — any email from `dev-portal@ins.twdcgrid.com`
- **Celebrating Disney** — any email from `notifications_disney@engage.mail.microsoft` or with "Celebrating Disney" as sender

Use OData `--filter` for server-side filtering where possible. For exclusions that OData can't handle (e.g., subject contains), filter client-side after fetching.

## Common Operations

- List unread: `outlook mail list --agent --filter "isRead eq false" --limit 20`
- Use `--agent` flag for structured JSON output
- Use OData `--filter` for server-side filtering (not client-side)

## Before Any Outlook Operation

Read `~/.claude/memory/tools/cli-universe.md` for shared auth infrastructure and common flags.

# Teams — Domain Knowledge

## Topic-based conversation table

When the user asks for **conversations around a specific topic** (e.g. “YouTube Masthead”, “Media360”, “Fivetran migration”), produce a table of the **most recent 10** messages where they were **mentioned or they discussed** that topic in Teams. Follow this workflow and use the table format below.

### 1. Search Teams

- **Tool:** Teams MCP (or teams-mcp-server CLI).
- **Query:** `"[TOPIC]" "Nasir, Sameul"` so results are both about the topic and mention the user (or where they posted).
- **Scope:** `from=0`, `size=10` (or fetch a few more to allow for dedup/same-thread).
- **Example:** MCP `mcp__teams__teams_search` with query `YouTube Masthead "Nasir, Sameul"`, size 10–15.

### 2. Resolve Channel / Meeting / Chat for Each Result

For each hit you need a **Channel** (or equivalent) and, when possible, a **Thread link**.

| Result type | How to resolve name & link |
|-------------|----------------------------|
| **Channel** | Use `teamName` and `channelName` from MCP search results. For the **Thread link** column, always use the `messageLink` URL from the MCP `teams_search` result — this links directly to the specific message/thread, not just the channel. Build the HYPERLINK as `=HYPERLINK(“messageLink_url”,”Open”)`. Only fall back to channel-level links if `messageLink` is unavailable. |
| **Meeting** | Match `conversationId` (threadId) to calendar: use CLI `teams --agent meeting list --days N` for a date range that includes the message date. Match `threadId` to get **subject** (meeting name). Show as **Meeting: [Subject]** (e.g. “Meeting: FiveTran Migration Sync”). No reliable deep link; use “—“ for Thread link. |
| **Group DM / 1:1** | If the conversation is in **favorites**, use CLI `teams --agent chat favorites` to get the favorite’s **displayName**. If not, use CLI `teams --agent message list --chat-id <conversationId>` and infer from participants (e.g. “Group chat (Person A, Person B, …)”). Thread link for chats: “—“ unless you have a known-good link. |

**User’s tenantId** (for links): from session/config (e.g. `56b731a8-a2ac-4c32-bf6b-616810e913c6`); use the same value used elsewhere for Teams links.

### 3. Thread Title and Message Title

- **Title of thread:** For channels, use the **root post** of the thread when known (e.g. “[Youtube Masthead FiveTran Emails]”) or a short topic line. For meetings/chats use “(Meeting chat)” or “(unknown)” if not available.
- **Title of message:** The **message preview/snippet** from the search result (the text of the post where the user was mentioned or replied).

### 4. Table Format

Produce **exactly** this table (chronological, **most recent first**; limit to the 10 most recent):

| Date | Channel | Thread link | Title of thread | Title of message | Owner |
|------|--------|-------------|------------------|------------------|--------|
| *MMM D, YYYY* | *Channel or “Meeting: Name” or “Group chat (A, B, ...)”* | *[Open channel] link or N/A* | *[Thread topic] or [Meeting chat] / [Unknown]* | *Message preview (truncate with ...)* | *Sender display name* |

**Mentions Catch-Up format** (extends the base table with 2 extra columns):

| Date | Channel | Thread link | Title of thread | Title of message | Owner | Your reply | Needs action? |
|------|---------|-------------|-----------------|------------------|-------|------------|---------------|

**Column rules:**

- **Date** — Message date from search `Time`, formatted as “Mon D, YYYY” (e.g. Mar 3, 2026).
- **Channel** — Resolved as in step 2 (channel name, meeting name, or group chat participants).
- **Thread link** — Clickable “Open” hyperlink for channels; “N/A” for meetings/chats with no link.
- **Title of thread** — Wrap in square brackets **only** when a Thread link is present (i.e. channel threads). For meetings, chats, and any row where Thread link is “N/A”, do **not** use brackets (e.g. “Meeting chat”, “1:1 chat”).
- **Your reply** — Summary of the user's most recent reply in that thread after the mention. “No reply found” if none exists.
- **Needs action?** — “Yes — unreplied” if no reply. “Maybe — [reason]” if replied but the question wasn't fully addressed. “No” if fully addressed.
- **Title of message** — Full preview from search; truncate long text with “...”.
- **Owner** — Sender of the message (From / display name).

### Default output: Google Sheet (single reusable sheet)

Always output to the **”Teams Mentions” tab** in the persistent Google Sheet below (not CSV) unless the user explicitly asks for CSV. Do **not** create a new tab each time — clear and overwrite the existing “Teams Mentions” tab.

**Sheet ID:** `1cT9qpNykuZ692UlQ1jufExH18_R7qwc38RXi-JDym9o`
**URI:** `doc://google/spreadsheet/1cT9qpNykuZ692UlQ1jufExH18_R7qwc38RXi-JDym9o`
**Link:** https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1cT9qpNykuZ692UlQ1jufExH18_R7qwc38RXi-JDym9o/edit
**Tab name:** `Teams Mentions`

**Google Sheet workflow:**
1. Clear existing data via `clear_spreadsheet_range` (range `Teams Mentions!A1:H100` or similar to cover previous data).
2. Write header row + new data via `write_spreadsheet_range` to `Teams Mentions!A1:H{n}`. For Topic Conversations (6 columns), use `A1:F{n}`. For Mentions Catch-Up (8 columns), use `A1:H{n}`.
3. For Thread link cells with a URL, use `=HYPERLINK(“url”,”Open”)` formula so the cell shows a clickable “Open” link.
4. For Thread link cells with no URL (meetings, chats), write plain text “N/A”.
5. Share the Google Sheet link with the user when done.

**CSV fallback rules** (only when user asks for CSV):
- Use only ASCII characters — no em dashes, curly quotes, or ellipsis characters. Use “N/A”, straight quotes, and “...” instead.
- Wrap any field containing commas, quotes, or newlines in double quotes.
- Escape double quotes inside fields by doubling them (“”).
- Use UTF-8 encoding with BOM (`\xEF\xBB\xBF` prefix) so Excel reads it correctly.

### 5. Sort Order

- Sort by **message date/time descending** (newest first).
- Within the same day, sort by **time descending**.
- Return only the **10 most recent** messages that match the topic + mention/discussion criteria.

### 6. Example Trigger Phrases

- “Conversations around [topic]”
- “Times someone mentioned me about [topic] in Teams”
- “Where did we discuss [topic] in Teams”
- “YouTube Masthead conversations” / “Media360 threads where I was mentioned”

When the user asks in this way, run the search with the topic and “Nasir, Sameul”, resolve channels/meetings/chats, then output the table in the format above with the 10 most recent rows in chronological order (most recent first).

### 7. @Mention Rule

@mention behavioral rules auto-load from `rules/teams.md`. See that file for the workflow.

### 8. Tools Summary (Hybrid CLI + MCP)

| Step | Tool | Type |
|------|------|------|
| Search | MCP: `mcp__teams__teams_search` with query + size | MCP (rich results: messageLink, conversationId, content) |
| Channel lookup | CLI: `teams --agent channel teams` → match by name | CLI |
| Meeting name | CLI: `teams --agent meeting list --days N` → match threadId to conversationId | CLI |
| Favorites (for chat names) | CLI: `teams --agent chat favorites` → match conversationId to displayName | CLI |
| Group chat participants | CLI: `teams --agent message list --chat-id <id>` → infer “Group chat (A, B, …)” from senders | CLI |
| People search | CLI: `teams --agent people search --query “Name”` → MRI = `8:orgid:{id}` | CLI |
| Send/reply | CLI: `teams --agent channel send` / `teams --agent channel reply` / `teams --agent message send` | CLI |
| Activity feed | MCP: `mcp__teams__teams_get_activity` with limit 200 | MCP (type filtering: mention vs message) |

---

## Mentions Catch-Up Workflow

When the user asks to **catch up on Teams mentions** (e.g., "what did I miss on Teams", "catch up on Teams", "teams mentions"), follow this workflow to produce a deduplicated, hyperlinked table of recent @mentions.

### Step-by-Step Process

1. **Pull activity feed**: MCP `mcp__teams__teams_get_activity` with `limit: 200`
2. **Filter mentions**: Keep only items where `type` = `mention`
3. **Filter by date**: Default to today + yesterday unless user specifies a range. Parse `createdDateTime` from each activity item.
4. **Resolve real message links**: For each mention, use MCP `mcp__teams__teams_search` with the sender's display name + key words from the `preview` text to find the actual message. Extract the `messageLink` field from the search result. **Never use `activityLink`** — activity feed links with `nr:system:clump:` in the conversationId are aggregated notification links, not direct message links.
5. **Resolve channel/meeting/chat**: Use CLI for resolution — `teams --agent channel teams` for channels, `teams --agent meeting list --days N` for meetings, `teams --agent chat favorites` / `teams --agent message list --chat-id <id>` for chats.
6. **Deduplicate**: Group by thread (`conversationId` prefix). Keep only the most recent mention per thread.
7. **Exclude non-actionable**: Skip automated bot messages, system notifications, and activity items without meaningful content.
8. **Check for user's reply**: For each mention, search `from:Sameul.Nasir@disney.com` + keywords from the mention in the same thread/channel (or use results already fetched). If a reply exists after the mention timestamp, note the reply content summary. If no reply found, mark as unreplied. When a reply exists but doesn't fully address the question asked, flag as "Maybe".
9. **Present table**: Use the Mentions Catch-Up table format (step 4 below) — includes "Your reply" and "Needs action?" columns beyond the base Topic Conversations format.

### Trigger Phrases

- "catch up on Teams"
- "what did I miss on Teams"
- "teams mentions"
- "what do I have to catch up on Teams"
- "who mentioned me on Teams"
- "Teams activity"
- "review my Teams mentions"

### Key Differences from Topic Conversations

| Aspect | Topic Conversations | Mentions Catch-Up |
|--------|-------------------|-------------------|
| **Source** | MCP `teams_search` with topic query | MCP `teams_get_activity` (activity feed) |
| **Filter** | Topic keyword + user name | `type: mention` + date range |
| **Scope** | Any message about a topic | Only direct @mentions of the user |
| **Dedup** | By thread (same topic) | By thread (same conversationId) |
| **Default date** | No date filter | Today + yesterday |

---

- **2026-03-03** [claude-code]: Added topic-based conversation table workflow (search, resolve channel/meeting/chat, table format, sort order). Teams MCP: see `mcp.json` and teams-mcp-server repo.
- **2026-03-18** [claude-code]: Added Mentions Catch-Up workflow (activity feed → filter mentions → resolve real links → deduplicate → table).
- **2026-03-23** [claude-code]: Migrated to hybrid CLI+MCP — CLI for writes/lookups (send, reply, delete, people, channels, meetings, favorites), MCP for reads (search with messageLink, activity feed with type filtering). Updated tools summary, resolution steps, MRI construction (`8:orgid:{id}`).
- **2026-03-25** [claude-code]: Added reply-check step (step 8) to Mentions Catch-Up workflow — searches for user's reply after each mention, adds "Your reply" and "Needs action?" columns. Updated Google Sheet range to 8 columns (A:H).

# Teams Workflow

## Hybrid Tool Rule

Teams operations use a **hybrid CLI + MCP** approach:

| Operation | Tool | Why |
|-----------|------|-----|
| **Writes** (send, reply, delete, edit) | CLI: `teams --agent` via Bash | Reliable, no SSE flakiness |
| **Lookups** (people, channels, meetings, favorites, user) | CLI: `teams --agent` via Bash | Structured JSON, fast |
| **Search** (full-text with messageLink, content) | MCP: `mcp__teams__teams_search` | CLI missing critical fields (messageLink, conversationId, content) |
| **Activity feed** (mentions with type filtering) | MCP: `mcp__teams__teams_get_activity` | CLI can't distinguish mention vs message types |

Always use `--agent` flag for structured JSON output. Add `--full` when you need all fields.

## Browser Auth

Teams uses the shared CLI Universe browser auth flow. If auth fails with a SingletonLock error or stale cache, always use `--no-cache`: `! teams auth login --no-cache`. See `memory/tools/cli-universe.md` for full troubleshooting (stale cache fix, SingletonLock removal, nuclear option).

## @Mention Rule

Always @mention people by name when sending or replying to Teams messages. Never send a plain-text name when an @mention is possible.

1. Look up each person via CLI: `teams --agent people search --query "Name"`
2. Construct MRI from the `id` field: `8:orgid:{id}` (e.g., `8:orgid:89137a4f-f562-4512-ba44-7cb69e97a1d7`)
3. Use `@[Display Name](mri)` syntax in the message
4. If replying to someone's message, @mention them in the reply

This applies to ALL Teams messages — not just the teams-thread skill.

## Editing Messages with @Mentions

Do NOT use `teams --agent message edit` to add or fix @mentions — it renders them as raw text (same bug as MCP). Instead, delete the broken message (`teams --agent message delete --chat-id <id> --message-id <id>`) and re-send via `teams --agent message send` or `teams --agent channel send`. Get the mention formatting right on the first send. When cc'ing people, always prefix with "cc: " before the @mentions.

## Thread Titles

Never wrap thread titles in **markdown bold**. Send titles as plain text. Only use formatting (bold, italic, etc.) when the user explicitly asks for it.

## Preserve User's Exact Wording

When the user provides the exact message text to send (including @-prefixes, punctuation, formatting), preserve it verbatim. Do not drop characters like "@" from "@Everyone" or reword the message. Send exactly what was requested.

## Mentions Catch-Up

When the user asks to "catch up on Teams", "what did I miss on Teams", "teams mentions", or similar, run the mentions catch-up workflow from `memory/domain/teams.md` (Mentions Catch-Up section). Key behavioral rules:

1. Use MCP `mcp__teams__teams_get_activity` (limit 200) to pull the activity feed — do NOT use `teams_search` as the primary source
2. Filter to `type: mention` items only, then filter by the user's requested date range (default: today + yesterday)
3. For each mention, use MCP `mcp__teams__teams_search` with the sender name + keywords from the preview to find the **real message link** (`messageLink` field) — never use `activityLink` from the activity feed (aggregated notification links are not direct message links)
4. Deduplicate by thread (same `conversationId` prefix) — keep only the most recent mention per thread
5. For channel/meeting/chat resolution, use CLI: `teams --agent channel teams` (channels), `teams --agent meeting list` (meetings), `teams --agent chat favorites` (chat names)
6. Exclude non-actionable items (automated bot messages, system notifications)
7. Present results in the standard table format from `memory/domain/teams.md`

## Jira Ticket Links in Messages

When including Jira ticket references in Teams messages (threads, replies, or self-chat drafts), always:

1. Use `--content-type html` flag on the send/reply command
2. Hyperlink each ticket ID using HTML anchor tags: `<a href="https://jira.disney.com/browse/DSACQ-XXXXX">DSACQ-XXXXX</a>`
3. Include the ticket summary after the link: `<a href="...">DSACQ-15221</a> - Hulu Media360 - Description`
4. Use `<ul><li>` for bullet lists (not markdown `-`)

Plain text `--content-type text` (the default) renders HTML tags as literal text. Always switch to `html` when the message contains links.

## Topic Conversations

When the user asks for conversations around a specific topic in Teams, read `~/.claude/memory/domain/teams.md` for the full workflow (search, resolve, table format, output sheet).

================
File: scripts/check-doc-sync.py
================
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Pre-commit hook: enforce documentation sync rules from CLAUDE.md.

Blocks commits that change trigger files (hooks, settings, mcp, skills, scripts)
without also updating the corresponding documentation targets.

Rules:
  0. Every commit must include README.md (unless README.md is the only file)
  1. hooks/ | settings.json | mcp.json  ->  mlflow/README.md
  2. skills/*/SKILL.md  ->  CLAUDE.md
  3. memory/ files added or deleted  ->  memory/memory.md
"""

import os
import re
import subprocess
import sys

SYNC_RULES = [
    (
        r"^(hooks/|settings\.json$|mcp\.json$)",
        "mlflow/README.md",
        "hooks/settings.json/mcp.json changed -> also update mlflow/README.md",
    ),
    (
        r"^skills/.*/SKILL\.md$",
        "CLAUDE.md",
        "skill definitions changed -> also update CLAUDE.md (Available Skills table)",
    ),
    (
        r"^(hooks/|settings\.json$)",
        "memory/tools/hooks.md",
        "hooks/settings.json changed -> also update memory/tools/hooks.md (hook architecture)",
    ),
    (
        r"^lessons/",
        "memory/memory.md",
        "lessons changed -> also update memory/memory.md index",
    ),
    (
        r"^evals/",
        "README.md",
        "evals/ changed -> also update README.md",
    ),
]


def check_sync_rules(
    staged: list[str], memory_added_deleted: list[str]
) -> list[str]:
    """Pure function: returns error messages for violated sync rules."""
    staged_set = set(staged)
    errors = []

    # Rule 0: README.md must be in every commit (unless it's the only file)
    non_readme = [f for f in staged if f != "README.md"]
    if non_readme and "README.md" not in staged_set and os.path.isfile("README.md"):
        errors.append(
            "every commit must include README.md (even a trivial edit)"
        )

    for pattern, target, message in SYNC_RULES:
        if not os.path.isfile(target):
            continue
        has_trigger = any(re.search(pattern, f) for f in staged if f != target)
        if has_trigger and target not in staged_set:
            errors.append(message)

    # Memory rule: only on add/delete, not modification
    if memory_added_deleted:
        if "memory/memory.md" not in staged_set and os.path.isfile("memory/memory.md"):
            errors.append(
                "memory files added/removed -> also update memory/memory.md index"
            )

    return errors


def get_staged_files() -> list[str]:
    """Return list of staged file paths (relative to repo root)."""
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["git", "diff", "--cached", "--name-only"],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True,
    )
    return [f for f in result.stdout.strip().splitlines() if f]


def get_memory_added_deleted() -> list[str]:
    """Return memory/ files that are staged as added or deleted."""
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["git", "diff", "--cached", "--name-only", "--diff-filter=AD", "--", "memory/"],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True,
    )
    return [f for f in result.stdout.strip().splitlines() if f]


def run_tests() -> bool:
    """Run pytest if test-relevant files are staged. Returns True if tests pass or are skipped."""
    test_triggers = re.compile(
        r"^(scripts/|hooks/|tests/|scripts/lib/)"
    )
    staged = get_staged_files()
    if not any(test_triggers.search(f) for f in staged):
        return True  # No test-relevant files changed, skip

    print("Running tests...", file=sys.stderr)
    result = subprocess.run(
        [sys.executable, "-m", "pytest", "tests/", "-q", "--tb=short"],
        capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30,
        cwd=os.path.expanduser("~/.claude"),
    )
    if result.returncode != 0:
        print("Tests failed!", file=sys.stderr)
        print("", file=sys.stderr)
        # Show just the failure summary, not full output
        for line in result.stdout.splitlines():
            if "FAILED" in line or "ERROR" in line or "short test summary" in line.lower():
                print(f"  {line}", file=sys.stderr)
            elif line.strip().startswith("E "):
                print(f"  {line}", file=sys.stderr)
        # Always show the last line (summary)
        last_line = result.stdout.strip().splitlines()[-1] if result.stdout.strip() else ""
        if last_line and "FAILED" not in last_line:
            print(f"  {last_line}", file=sys.stderr)
        print("", file=sys.stderr)
        print(
            "Fix failing tests, or bypass with: git commit --no-verify",
            file=sys.stderr,
        )
        return False
    return True


def main() -> int:
    staged = get_staged_files()
    if not staged:
        return 0

    memory_ad = get_memory_added_deleted()
    errors = check_sync_rules(staged, memory_ad)

    if errors:
        print("Documentation sync check failed!", file=sys.stderr)
        print("", file=sys.stderr)
        for err in errors:
            print(f"  - {err}", file=sys.stderr)
        print("", file=sys.stderr)
        print(
            "Stage the missing doc updates, or bypass with: git commit --no-verify",
            file=sys.stderr,
        )
        return 1

    if not run_tests():
        return 1

    return 0


if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())
