129 tracked files total. 25 artifacts tracked. Transient data (history, debug, session state, local overrides) is gitignored.

## Core components

### `CLAUDE.md` — Global instructions

The main control file. Claude Code reads this at the start of every session. Contains only behavioral rules (~80 lines) that apply every session. Stable rules (memory system, Jira workflow, testing conventions) have been extracted to `rules/` for guaranteed auto-loading:

- **Memory system pointer** — references `rules/memory-system.md` for core rules, keeps only maintenance/reorganize workflow
- **System routing intelligence** — detects Claude Code vs Cortex Code via `CORTEX_SESSION_ID` env var, recommends the right system for the task
- **Skill routing & loading rules** — how to match user requests to skills, points to `memory/domain/skills-catalog.md`
- **CLAUDE.md versioning** — save/diff/rollback via git tags
- **Failure pattern awareness** — silently apply lessons from Claude's 32 documented past mistakes
- **Known issues awareness** — silently apply workarounds for environment/tool problems
- **Reference files pointer table** — tells Claude where on-demand content lives (trace workflows, skill catalog, known issue procedures)
- **Documentation sync rules** — what to update when modifying files

### `settings.json` — Model config, hooks, environment

```jsonc
{
  "env": {
    "CLAUDE_CODE_USE_BEDROCK": "1",         // Route through AWS Bedrock
    "AWS_REGION": "us-west-2",
    "AWS_PROFILE": "twdc-bedrock-central",
    "ANTHROPIC_MODEL": "global.anthropic.claude-opus-4-6-v1",
    "MLFLOW_CLAUDE_TRACING_ENABLED": "true", // MLflow session tracing
    "MLFLOW_TRACKING_URI": "http://127.0.0.1:5001",
    "CLAUDE_AUTOCOMPACT_PCT_OVERRIDE": "50"  // Compact at 50% (between tasks, not mid-task)
  },
  "hooks": { ... },                          // SessionStart, PreCompact, PreToolUse, Stop hooks
  "statusLine": { ... },                     // Custom status bar
  "enabledPlugins": { ... }
}
```

> **Important:** All environment variables must be under the `"env"` key. Claude Code ignores variables under an `"environment"` key.

**Hooks:**
- `SessionStart` — runs `git-auto-pull.sh` (auto-pulls updates from claude-settings repo if working tree is clean), `inject-memory.sh` (loads memory index, failure patterns, known issues, last session summary, and compact state into context), `ensure-mlflow.sh` (starts MLflow server if not running), `health-check.py --mode session-start` (checks MLflow, Docker, AWS creds, cost tracking — warns in-context if issues found), and `sync-traces.sh` (auto-syncs `traces.csv` edits back to MLflow if the file was modified since last sync)
- `PreCompact` — runs `save-compact-state.py` before context compaction to preserve working state (recent user requests + files being worked on) so it survives compaction
- `UserPromptSubmit` — runs `plan-consultation-check.sh` to enforce Plan Consultation rule (reminds Claude to read failure patterns, known issues, and relevant memory before drafting plans)
- `PreToolUse` (Bash) — runs `check-aws-ttl.sh` before every Bash call to ensure AWS credentials are valid
- `PreToolUse` (all) — runs `check-ms-auth-ttl.sh` before every tool call to check Teams/Outlook OAuth token TTL; Teams uses headless refresh, Outlook requires browser login
- `PreToolUse` (Write|Edit) — runs `enforce-plan-consultation.py` to block plan file writes (`plans/*.md`) that lack an `## Informed By` section with actual content
- `Stop` — MLflow trace capture + cost tracking (transcript parsing → CSV + MLflow tags) + session summary (`.last-session.md` for next-session continuity) + cost row validation (`health-check.py --mode stop`, macOS notification on failure) + maintenance checks (`maintain-check.py`) when Claude finishes

### `mcp.json` — MCP server connections

Six MCP servers:

| Server | Transport | Purpose |
|--------|-----------|---------|
| `jira` | SSE (`localhost:3000`) | Jira Cloud via Docker container |
| `confluence-disney` | stdio (uv + fastmcp) | Confluence pages — read/search/update |
| `universal-doc` | stdio (uv) | Google Docs, Sheets, Slides — read/write/create |
| `mlflow-mcp` | stdio (uv) | MLflow experiment tracking and model registry |
| `teams` | stdio (`teams-mcp-server/bin/run.sh`) | Microsoft Teams — search + activity feed only (writes/lookups moved to CLI in hybrid setup) |
| `notion` | HTTP (`mcp.notion.com/mcp`) | Notion pages, databases, tasks, comments |

> **Note:** The Notion MCP server is configured at the user level via `claude mcp add` (not in `mcp.json`).

### `hooks/check-aws-ttl.sh` — AWS credential lifecycle

Runs before every Bash tool call. Checks AWS credential TTL and handles refresh:

- **Credentials valid** (TTL > 5 min) — pass through
- **Expiring soon** (TTL < 5 min) — attempt proactive refresh
- **Expired** — block the tool call and trigger refresh

Refresh strategies (tried in order): tmux popup, silent refresh, iTerm2/Terminal.app new tab, manual fallback.

### `hooks/check-ms-auth-ttl.sh` — Teams/Outlook token lifecycle

Runs before every tool call. Checks Microsoft OAuth token TTL for both Teams and Outlook CLIs:

- **Tokens valid** (TTL > 5 min) — pass through
- **Expiring soon** (TTL < 5 min) — attempt proactive refresh
- **Expired** — block the tool call and trigger refresh

Refresh strategies differ by CLI:
- **Teams**: headless `auth refresh` (no browser) → tmux popup → terminal tab → manual fallback
- **Outlook**: tmux popup with `auth login` (no headless option) → terminal tab → manual fallback

### `statusline.sh` — Custom status bar

Displays a single-line status bar with:

```
repo branch │ S:n M:n ?:n │ $cost duration (api time) │ +n -n │ Model [vim] (agent) version @session  aws TTL  ctx n% (tokens)
```

Includes context window urgency indicators (warning at 70%, critical at 90%) and AWS credential TTL countdown.

## Skills catalog

Skills are invoked with `/skill-name` in Claude Code. Each lives in `skills/{name}/SKILL.md`. Every skill includes Examples (2+ concrete scenarios), Guidelines (constraints, edge cases), and validated `allowed-tools` declarations per [Anthropic best practices](https://github.com/anthropics/skills).

### Jira & project management

| Skill | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| `/jira-ticket-finder` | Parameterized Jira ticket finder — presets: `active`, `completed`, `report` (per-board + FiveTran Migration breakout with risk analysis), `hulu-m360`, `custom`. Scripts in `query.py`, `query_report.py`, and `query_hulu_m360.py` |
| `/update-atlassian-token` | Validate, auto-detect, and apply Atlassian PAT tokens (Jira/Confluence) with persistent storage and expiry checks |

### Google Workspace & productivity

| Skill | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| `/workspace-references` | Display tracked artifacts (21 Docs/Sheets/Slides), PRDs, document/slides templates, Confluence key pages — or save new artifacts. Health check now detects legacy commands/ files |
| `/confluence-page-builder` | Build Confluence pages (requirements docs, design docs, mappings tables) using DSSDSA templates with storage format HTML. Asks which Confluence page first, then what to build when invoked without arguments. Interactive step-by-step intake for requirements preset. Presets: `requirements`, `design`, `mappings`, `update` |

### Strategy & review

| Skill | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| `/building-unicorn-company` | Strategic advisor for building billion-dollar SaaS companies |
| `/product-growth-expert` | B2C SaaS growth strategy expert (Sean Ellis, Brian Balfour, Andrew Chen, Elena Verna, Nir Eyal frameworks) |
| `/dashboard-designer` | Dashboard design framework synthesized from 12 data visualization books |
| `/health-check` | Full system diagnostics + Jira auto-repair — infra, MCP servers, AWS creds, cost tracking, skill validation |
| `/ab-test-claude-md` | Set up and track A/B tests comparing CLAUDE.md versions |
| `/skill-creator` | Create new skills, improve existing skills, run evals, benchmark performance, optimize descriptions |

### Databricks

| Skill | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| `/unity-databricks` | Monitor DLT pipelines (read-only), browse Unity Catalog, run SQL queries via SQL Statements API. Key schemas: `acquisition_de_prod.publish`, `acquisition_de_prod.build` |

### Teams

| Skill | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| `/teams-thread` | Create a Teams channel thread with reply and tagged people, with self-notes preview before posting. Hybrid CLI+MCP: CLI for writes/lookups, MCP for search |

### cli-universe (9 CLIs installed from [AIAdvance/cli-universe](https://github.twdcgrid.net/AIAdvance/cli-universe))

| `udoc-cli` | Universal Doc across Google, Microsoft, and local providers |
| `unvrs-cli` | Universal dispatcher + plugin management (Databricks, GitHub CLI, LaunchDarkly, Terraform) |


## Setup

### 1. Clone and symlink

```bash
git clone https://github.twdcgrid.net/sameul-nasir/claude-settings.git
# Back up any existing ~/.claude if needed
ln -sf "$(pwd)/claude-settings" ~/.claude
```

### 2. AWS Bedrock configuration

This setup routes Claude Code through AWS Bedrock rather than the Anthropic API directly. You need:

- AWS CLI configured with a `twdc-bedrock-central` profile
- The `ca` credential helper installed at `~/.local/bin/ca`
- Valid AWS credentials (the hook handles refresh automatically)

The relevant environment variables are set in `settings.json` under `env`.

### 3. MCP servers

**Jira** — runs as a Docker container exposing SSE on `localhost:3000`:
```bash
# See /health-check skill (Jira Auto-Repair section) for the exact Docker setup
# Requires JIRA_URL, JIRA_EMAIL, JIRA_API_TOKEN environment variables
```

**Confluence** — runs via `uv` using a local `confluence-mcp-server` repo:
```bash
# Clone the confluence-mcp-server repo to ~/confluence-mcp-server
# Requires a .env file with Confluence credentials
```

**Google Workspace (universal-doc)** — runs via `uv` from a local `universal-doc-mcp` directory:
```bash
# Clone the universal-doc-mcp repo to ~/universal-doc-mcp
# Requires Google OAuth credentials
```

**MLflow** — runs via `uv` with the `mlflow[mcp]` package:
```bash
# The ensure-mlflow.sh SessionStart hook auto-starts the server.
# To start manually (note: 4 slashes for absolute path):
mlflow server --host 127.0.0.1 --port 5001 --backend-store-uri sqlite:////Users/sameul.nasir/mlflow.db
```

**Notion** — configured at the user level (not in `mcp.json`):
```bash
claude mcp add notion --transport http --url https://mcp.notion.com/mcp
# Requires a Notion integration token
```

### 4. Notion commands

`commands/Notion/` contains 10 slash commands for direct Notion operations — `create-page`, `search`, `database-query`, `create-task`, `find`, `create-database-row`, and a `tasks/` sub-group (`build`, `plan`, `setup`, `explain-diff`). These are gitignored because they're installed from the Notion plugin marketplace (`plugins/marketplaces/notion-plugin-marketplace/`), not authored in this repo.

### 5. Local settings

`settings.local.json` (gitignored) contains machine-specific permission allowlists for MCP tools and Bash commands. Create your own based on the tools you want to auto-approve.

### 6. MLflow tracing

Session tracing is enabled via `settings.json` environment variables and the `Stop` hooks. Supporting scripts live in the home directory:

| Script | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `~/export_traces.py` | Export traces from SQLite to `~/.claude/traces.csv` (denormalized, one row per trace) |
| `~/sync_traces.py` | Sync edited tags from CSV back to SQLite (INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE changed tags) |
| `~/tag_traces.py` | Interactive CLI to tag, bookmark, and view session traces |
| `~/refresh_failure_patterns.py` | Regenerate `memory/domain/failure-patterns.md` from tagged traces |
| `~/refresh_saved_traces.py` | Regenerate `memory/domain/saved-traces.md` from bookmarked traces |
| `~/refresh_known_issues.py` | Regenerate `memory/domain/known-issues.md` from traces + manual JSON |

**Trace tagging workflow**:
1. `python3 ~/export_traces.py` — export traces to CSV
2. Edit `~/.claude/traces.csv` (spreadsheet or ask Claude in-session)
3. `python3 ~/sync_traces.py` — sync changes back + auto-refresh memory files

Cost tracking is handled by `hooks/capture-cost.py` (Stop hook) which parses session transcript JSONL files for token usage, computes USD cost from Bedrock pricing, and writes to `~/.claude/cost-log.csv` + MLflow trace tags. Includes a 2s delay to catch the final trace (race condition fix) and a retroactive sweep that tags orphaned last-traces from prior sessions. See `mlflow/README.md` for details.

## Memory system

Claude Code maintains a structured knowledge base in `memory/` that persists across sessions.

### How it works

1. `memory/memory.md` is the index — read at session start
2. New knowledge is written to the appropriate file immediately (not batched)
3. Each entry contains: date, what, why
4. After any memory change, Claude auto-commits and pushes to this repo

### File organization

| Path | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `memory.md` | Master index with one-line descriptions |
| `general.md` | Cross-project facts, preferences, environment setup |
| `domain/{topic}.md` | Domain-specific knowledge (one file per topic) |
| `tools/{tool}.md` | Tool configs, CLI patterns, workarounds |

### Maintenance

Say "reorganize memory" to trigger a cleanup: dedup, merge, split, re-sort, and reindex.

## Failure patterns & trace management

### Trace tagging

The primary way to tag traces is via `~/.claude/traces.csv`:

```bash
# Export traces to CSV (default: last 30 days)
python3 ~/export_traces.py
python3 ~/export_traces.py --all        # All traces
python3 ~/export_traces.py --days 90    # Last 90 days

# Edit the CSV (spreadsheet or ask Claude in-session to tag)
# Editable columns: failure_mode, category, description, prevention_rule, severity, save

# Sync changes back to SQLite
python3 ~/sync_traces.py                # Apply changes
python3 ~/sync_traces.py --dry-run      # Preview without writing
```

The sync script auto-runs the relevant refresh scripts when tags change.

The interactive CLI (`tag_traces.py`) is still available for viewing traces and terminal-based tagging.

### Failure patterns

Failures from past sessions are stored in `memory/domain/failure-patterns.md`, grouped by category. Patterns with a specific `prevention_rule` tag are displayed verbatim. Legacy patterns (only `failure_mode`, no `prevention_rule`) fall back to generic rules and appear in an "Uncategorized" section.

At session start, Claude reads this file and silently applies prevention rules when working on similar task categories.

Manual refresh:
```bash
python3 ~/refresh_failure_patterns.py
```

### Saved traces & skill distillation

Good sessions can be bookmarked by setting `save` to `true` in `traces.csv`, or via the interactive CLI:

```bash
# Bookmark via CLI
python3 ~/tag_traces.py --save

# View bookmarked traces
python3 ~/tag_traces.py --saved-only

# Inspect a specific trace
python3 ~/tag_traces.py --view <trace_id>

# Filter by category
python3 ~/tag_traces.py --category jira
```

The index at `memory/domain/saved-traces.md` auto-refreshes on bookmark. Manual refresh:
```bash
python3 ~/refresh_saved_traces.py
```

## Maintenance & testing

### Health checks

**Session start** (`health-check.py --mode session-start`) — runs automatically at the start of every session. Checks MLflow, Docker/Jira, AWS credentials, cost CSV integrity, and cost anomalies. Silent when healthy. Warnings are injected into Claude's context so Claude tells you immediately.

**Session end** (`health-check.py --mode stop`) — runs after `capture-cost.py`. Validates the cost row just written isn't empty/malformed. Sends a macOS notification if something's wrong.

**On demand** (`/health-check`) — full diagnostic including MCP server dependency checks, git sync verification, and cost trends.

### A/B testing CLAUDE.md

CLAUDE.md controls all of Claude's behavior. When making changes, use the built-in
versioning system to compare results and roll back if needed.

**Save before making changes:**
> "save my CLAUDE.md as before-trace-rewrite"

This creates a git tag (`claude-md/before-trace-rewrite`) you can always return to.

**Make your changes, run a few sessions, then compare:**
> "diff CLAUDE.md against before-trace-rewrite"

**If the new version is worse, roll back:**
> "rollback CLAUDE.md to before-trace-rewrite"

**Other commands:**
> "list my CLAUDE.md versions" — shows all saved versions + the auto-checkpoint
> "rollback CLAUDE.md" (no label) — restores from the last auto-checkpoint

**How auto-checkpoints work:**
Every session start that passes health checks, the current commit SHA is saved to
`.claude-md-checkpoint`. This gives you a "last known good" fallback without
any manual action.

**Emergency rollback (when Claude itself is broken):**
If CLAUDE.md is so broken that Claude can't function, run from your terminal:
```bash
~/.claude/scripts/emergency-rollback.sh
```
This restores CLAUDE.md from the last auto-checkpoint.

### Documentation sync enforcement

A git pre-commit hook (`scripts/check-doc-sync.py`) enforces the Documentation
Sync Rules from CLAUDE.md. **Every commit must include README.md** (even a
trivial edit), unless README.md is the only file being committed. Additional
rules: hooks/settings/mcp changes require mlflow/README.md, skill changes
require CLAUDE.md, and memory file adds/deletes require memory/memory.md.
Commits missing required targets are blocked with a message showing what's missing.

The memory index rule only fires on file add/delete — auto-refreshed files
(failure-patterns.md, saved-traces.md, known-issues.md) don't trigger it.

Bypass with `git commit --no-verify` (manual terminal only — Claude Code
instructions prohibit `--no-verify`).

### Skill test framework

Validates all 21 skills with static checks (YAML front-matter, required fields, file references, MCP tool config, evaluation JSON, skills-catalog sync) and smoke tests (Docker/container status, template files, dependency skills, integration dirs).

```bash
python3 ~/.claude/scripts/test-skills.py              # All tests
python3 ~/.claude/scripts/test-skills.py --static-only # No runtime checks
python3 ~/.claude/scripts/test-skills.py --skill name  # Single skill
```

Exit code 0 if no FAILs. WARNs and SKIPs don't affect exit code.

### Maintenance checks

**Stop hook** (`maintain-check.py`) — runs at end of every session. Read-only, <2 seconds, always exits 0. Warns about:
- Memory index vs files on disk mismatches
- Auto-generated files older than 7 days
- Same-day duplicate changelog entries
- README.md directory tree drift (files on disk not listed, or listed files missing)

**Weekly cron** (`maintain-weekly.py`) — runs Sundays at 9 AM via launchd. Auto-fixes:
1. Consolidates same-day changelog entries
2. Refreshes auto-generated memory files (failure-patterns, saved-traces, known-issues)
3. Validates and fixes memory index
4. Runs static skill validation
5. Commits and pushes changes

```bash
python3 ~/.claude/scripts/maintain-weekly.py           # Full run
python3 ~/.claude/scripts/maintain-weekly.py --dry-run  # Preview changes
```

The launchd plist is at `~/Library/LaunchAgents/com.claude-code.maintain-weekly.plist` (not checked into git — machine-specific paths).

## Adapting this for your own setup

1. Fork this repo
2. Replace project-specific references (DSACQ, MEOW, QMDS board names, sprint names) with your own
3. Remove or replace MCP server configs for tools you don't use
4. Update `CLAUDE.md` with your own skill catalog and preferences
5. Build your own memory files as you work — the system is self-maintaining once the rules are in `CLAUDE.md`
